               - 注意 Did you bring the textbook? -- No,I didn't bring it. 你带了课本吗，我没有带课本
                  - one 和 it 都可以替代前文出现过的单数名词
                  - 但是 one 是指同一类的
                  - it 是限定，且没有修饰语的时候使用
            - 加修饰语
               - I lost my umbrella yesterday;I must buy a new one. 我昨天丢了雨伞，我必须买把新的雨伞
               - These boots have worn out I need to buy some new ones. 这些鞋子已经穿破了，我需要买些新的鞋子
               - I like that picture -- I mean the third one from the left. 我喜欢那幅画，我指的是从左边的第三幅
                  - 因为这里限定是限定的 the third，而不是准确的那幅画，所以用 one
               - the guitar is similar to the one I have. 这个吉他和我的很相似
                  - I have 是修饰的作用，不能用 it，因为 it 需要在限定且没有修饰的情况使用
                  - 所以这里用 one，但是前文有重复吉它所以用 one
                  - 但是又限定了我有的吉他，所以加 the，最终是 the one
            - 注意：one 不可代替不可数名词
               - He likes white wine better than red (wine).
                  - 因为 酒是不可数，所以不能用 one 代替
                  - 因为前文出现过 酒了，所以可以省略
            - 惯用表现
               - She is nurse and mother all in one to the orphans. 他是孤儿的母亲和护士（他是护士和母亲都在一个人身上在孤儿身上）
               - They left by/in ones and twos. 他们三三两两地离开了
               - They came,one and all,to welcome him. 他们全体都来欢迎他
                  - one and all 是为了修饰 They came
               - The teacher interviewed the students one by one. 老师逐一地对学生面试（老师对学生一个接着一个面试）
               - I,for one,do not agree. 就我个人来说不同意

   - both/all
      - 概念
         - both 用于二者；all 用于三者或以上；both/all 在beV动词之后，一般动词之前
         - both 和 not 结合 解释为 “并非两者都”；all 和 not 结合 解释为 并非全都
      - 例子
         - Both of my parents are happy about the result. 我父母两位对这个结果都很高兴
         - All (the) villagers knew of the accident. 所有的村民知道这个事故（这里 All 充当形容词）
            - All of the villagers knew of the accident. 所有村民知道这个事故（这里 All 充当代名词作主词，毕竟 of 前后都应该是名词）
            - The villagers all knew of the acident. 村民都知道这个事故（这里 all 充当同谓语，即充当了 The villagers）
         - 注意 know 可以直接根名词，这样体现是自己亲自知道的
         - 如果 know 加介词 再加名词，这样 know 变成了不及物动词，体现出是间接知道的
      - all + 单数名词 => 表“全体”
         - It rained all afternoon. 雨下了整个下午
         - All the town(=>The whole town) was destroyed. 整个镇都被破坏了
         - they jogged all the way. 他们整个路都是慢跑的
      - all + 抽象名词/身体部位之复数
         - The lady was all smiles. 这个女人满脸都是笑容
         - She was all ears. 她听力好（她全身都是耳朵，表明听力好）
         - all thumbs 笨手笨脚（所有都是大拇指，大拇指不灵活，所以不灵活，所以翻译为 笨手笨脚）
      - all 的惯用表现
         - There are 700 boys and girls in all in our school. 我们学校全部有700个学生（in all 全部；一共）
         - He ate the meat,bone and all. 他连同肉和骨头都吃了
         - We have all but finished the work. 我们几乎要完成了所有工作
            - all but = almost
            - all but “所有但是”这样理解那就是 almost
      - at all
         - 意思，语境
            - 全然 => 用于否定句
            - 究竟 => 用于疑问句
            - 既然 => 用于条件句（if子句)
         - 疑问
            - I wasn't surprised at all. 我不全然讶异
            - Do you know her at all? 你究竟认识她吗
            - If you learn English at all,learn it well. 既然你要学英语，学好它
            - For all her efforts,she failed. 尽管她很努力，但还是失败了
               - 这里的 all 是 adj. 用于修饰 her efforts
               - For all 可以替换为 In spite of
      - some/any
         - 表示“一些”
            - 用于肯定句中 => some
            - 否定，疑问，条件句中 => any
            - 例子
            - I need some coins. Have you got any?
            - Please lend me some money if you have any.
         - some => 表“某个”，any => 表“任何一个...都...”
            - How about having dinner at some good restaurant? 在某个好的餐厅吃晚饭怎样
            - Any of the magazines will do. 杂志的任何一本都可以读
         - some 用于疑问句
            - 表示邀请或请求的疑问句，或当说话者希望得到对方肯定的答案的时候 用 some
               - Would you like some coffee? 你想来些咖啡吗（这里是邀请）
               - If you eat some cabbage,I'll take you to the park. 如果你吃了些洋白菜，我会带你去公园（这里是希望对方肯定回答）
         - some 及 any 的副词用法
            - some（大约）；any（一点点<也>...）
               - Some forty people were present at the party. 大约40个人出席了这个派对
               - I can't wait any longer. 我不能再等一下子了
               - It's not any too big for you. 对你来说一点也不会太大
         - 惯用表现
            - I hope to visit London some day. 我某天希望参观伦敦
               - one day 某一天（可用于 过去式 或 未来式）
               - some day 某一天（只能用于未来式）
            - Let's discus it some other day. 改天讨论它吧
            - We'll call on him in any case. 我们无论如何都会拜访他
            - He was determined to finish the work at any lost. 他不惜任何代价都决定完成这个工作
               - at any lost 任何的损失下
            - Correct mistakes,if any. 如果有任何错，纠正错误
            - There is little water,if any. 如果有任何的水，也几乎很少（if there is any of water 缩写？)
      - other/another
         - 一般用法
            - 我不喜欢这个，请给我看另一个
               - I don't like this one;please show me the other.（这里 the other，the 限定另外一部分，因为 other 没有用复数，所以限定另一个，即一共两个）
               - I don't like this one;please show me the another.（这里 another，表明给我看另外一个，但是另外一个没有限定一定是两者的，所以总数不明）
            - Would you like another piece of pie? 你要另外再来一块派吗（一共有不确定的数目）
         - 列举
            - I have two sisters: one is married and the other isn't. 我有两个姐妹，一个结婚了，另一个没有结婚（the other 限定了另一个）
            - I have three sisters: one is sociable,but the others are too shy. 我有三个结婚，一个善于交际，而另两个太腼腆（the others 限定其它所有，是复数）
            - 注意
               - 数量为三时：one-another-the other（区分三个不同的对象）
               - 数量为四时：one-another-another-the other（区分四个不同的对象）
               - I have three young friends:one is eight years old,another is ten,and the other is twelve.
                  - 我有三个朋友，一个是8岁，另一个是10岁，最后一个是12岁
               - some of the club members came on time,but the others were all late. 俱乐部的一些成员准时到来了，其它全都迟到了
               - some of people are good at dancing and others aren't.（因为没有限定范围，所以用 others 不用 the others）
               - She hung her raincoat the hook and her umbrella on one another 她挂起了她的雨衣在挂勾上，雨伞挂在另一个挂勾上
                  - 第二个挂勾用 one 代替 hook，因为不清楚多少个挂勾所以没有限定，所以用 one another
               - 注意
                  - 未列举完
                     - some...,and some...（可数，不可数）
                     - some...,and others...（可数）
                  - 已列举完
                     - some...,and the rest...（可数，不可数）
                     - some...,and the others...（可数）
      - 惯用表现
         - I have a black cat and a white one:the one(->former) likes to play,and the other(->other) sleeps most of the day. 
            - 我有一只黑猫和一只白猫，一只喜欢玩耍，另一只几乎整天在睡觉
         - To know is one thing,and to teach is quite another. 了解是一回事，教别人知识是另外的一回事
         - They shouted each other. 他们彼此吼叫（each other 彼此）
         - We introduced one another at the welcoming party. 我们在欢迎会上介绍彼此（one other 彼此）
         - 注意
            - each other 和 one other 都是彼此的意思
         - The restaurant seved dishes one after another. 餐厅一道道上菜（菜不止两道，所以 用 another）
         - The two girls rowed the boat one after the other. 两个女孩轮流划船（一个在另一个之后划）
 
         - On (the) one hand we look for excitement,but on the other (hand),we look for peace in mind,
            - 一方面我们寻找刺激，但在另一方面,我们寻找心灵平和
      - each/every（每一）
         - 概念
            - each 二者以上各的各个或各人；代名词，形容词，副词
            - every 三者以上之每个；形容词
         - 举例
            - On each side of the street there were policemen. 在马路的每边都有警察
            - These hats cost 10 dollars each. 这些帽子每顶要10美元（这里的 each 作副词）
            - There are two books in his bag and each book is carefully wrapped in colorful paper. 两本书在他的书里，每本都细心地用有色的纸包装
               - 注意这里的三单，这里 each 注重个体
            - Every student has his favorite subject. 每个学生都有他的喜欢的学科
               - 注意这里的三单，这里 every 注重个体
               - every 接单数名词，通常用 his 表明它的所有格
            - Every dog and cat has his likes and dislikes. 每只狗和猫有它喜欢的和不喜欢的
            - 注意
               - every 和 each 都可以 + 单数名词 + 单数动词（注重个体）
      - every + 抽象名词（一切的）
            - I have every reason to believe it. 我有相信他的充分的理由
               - 这里的 every reason 充当整体
            - She showed me every kindness. 她极其所能地对我热心/仁慈
               - 这里的 every kindness 充当整体
      - every
         - 概念
            - every + 基数 + 复数名词（每隔...）
            - every + 序数 + 单数名词
         - 举例
            - 情况1
               - ABCDE（假设这几个字母为相邻的年数）
               - The Olympics are held every four years. 奥林匹克每四年举办一次
                   - 注重：ABCD 为一个单位
               - The Olympics are held every fourth year.奥林匹克每四年举办一次
                   - 注重：从 A 数数，数到第四个即 E
            - 情况2
               - I come here every other week. 我每隔一周来这一次（因为隔了一周，其实就是每两周来一次）
               - I come here every two weeks. 我两周来一次（来的那次是包含在这两周内的）
      - either / neither
         - 概念1
            - either 两者中任一都...（随便一个的肯定）
            - neither 两者中任一都不...（两者的否定）
            - 举例
               1. Either of the two answers will do. 两个回答的任意一个都可以
                  - 这里的 either 作 代名词
               2. 注意：Any of the three answers will do.
                  - 因为用了any，所以是 三者以上的任一，包含三者
               3. I can write with either hand. 我可以以任意一只手写字
                  - 这里的 either 作形容词
                  - 因为只有两只手，所以用 either 而不用 any
               4. I don't like either of the men. 这两个人的任意一个我都不喜欢
                  - 这里的 either 作代名词
               5. We passed two gas stations,but neither of them was open. 我经过了两个加油站，但它们都不是开放的
                  - 注意单数动词的使用，这里用的 was
               6. Neither of the titles is suitable for the essay. 这两个短文都不适合这篇短文
         - 概念2 
            - either /neither （也不）
            - 举例
               - Bill didn't come to the party,and Jack didn't either. 比利没来派对，杰克也没有来
               - Bill didn't come to the party,and neither did Jack. 比利没来派对，杰克也没有来（否定提前，应用倒装）
               - 注意：Bill came to the party, and Jack did,too. 比利没来派对，杰克也没来
               - 注意：Bill came to the party, so did Jack. 比利没来派对，杰克也没来（这里 so 解释成“如此”，且是副词，所以倒装句）
               - If you do not go,neither will I. 如果你不去，我也不会去
                  - 主句使用 未来式时，条件句用 一般现在式，所以这里的一般现在式表未来（所以看起来两边的时态不一样，实际上从意思来讲是一样的）

      - no / none
         - no + 单数名词/复数名词
            - no = not a/an/any
            - He has no money. 他没有钱 = He doesn't have any money.
            - She has no children. 她没有孩子
            - The policeman arrived in no time. 警察立刻就出现了（警察在没有时间之内到达）
         - not => 不~；no => 绝非~
            - He is not a musician. 他不是个音乐人
            - I am no thief. 我绝非是贼
               - I am by no means a thief.（by no means “绝非”）
         - none（无一）
            - none + 单数动词/复数动词
            - None of us agree with you. 我们没有一个同意你
            - None of us were(=>was) against the proposal. 我们之中没有一个人反对这个提案
               - “us”是可数的，所以用 were
               - 这里的 against 是介词
            - None of the information is useful. 没有一条信息是有用的
               - information 不可数，所以用 is
            - It's none of your business. 不关你的事/多管闲事
         - somebody ~ / something ~
            - somebody + 形容词
               - 其它的
                  - other + 名词
                  - else
                     - 疑问词 + else
                     - 放在 somebody... 等的后面
               - Will somebody else be present? 还有任何其它人要出席吗
            - 所有格 -> ~body's
               - Everybody's business is nobody's business. 所有人的事就是没有人的事
            - 特殊表现
               - He thinks he is somebody. 他以为他很了不起
               - If you want to be anybody,you must work hard. 如果你想成为某个人，你必须努力工作
            - 惯用表现
               - He is a lawyer or something. 他是律师类的人物
                  - Are you crazy or something? 你是疯了还是怎样
               - He would not go with (me) for anything. 他怎么样也不根我去
               - Peter isn't called a playboy for nothing. He had one girlfriend after another.
                  - 皮特被叫做花花公子不是没有道理的，他在另一个女朋友之后有了一个女朋友
                  - 皮特被叫做花花公子不是没有道理的，他交了一个女朋友后又交了女朋友
               - He did nothing but laugh. 他只会笑（他什么都没有做，但他笑了）
               - I had nothing to do with the accident. 我和这次意外无关
                  - I had much to do with ... 我和...很有关
                  - I had little to do with ... 我和...有一点关
               - He is nothing but a fool. 他就是个笨蛋（他什么都不是，但就是个笨蛋）


* 时态
   - 时态是由 时间 和 状态组合而成的
      - 时间：过去，现在，未来
      - 状态：简单式，进行式，完成式，完成进行式

   - 格式
      - 简单式
         - 现在式 She writes a letter.
         - 过去式 She wrote a letter.
         - 未来式 She will write a letter.
      - 进行式 beV + Ving
         - 现在进行式 She is writing a letter.
         - 过去进行式 She was writing a letter.
         - 未来进行式 She will be writing a letter.
      - 完成式 have/has/had + p.p.
         - 现在完成式 She has written a letter.
         - 过去完成式 She had written a letter.
         - 未来完成式 She will have written a letter.
      - 完成进行式 has/have/had + being + p.p.
         - 现在完成进行式 She has been writing a letter.
         - 过去完成进行式 She had been writinga letter.
         - 未来完成进行式 She will have been writing a letter.
   - 举例
      - Everything is in order. 每样东西是有序的
      - Everything is out of order. 每样东西是无序的
      - Joe owns a house by the sea. Joe 有楼在海边的房子

   - 时态
      1. 简单式
         1. 表习惯
            - I always drink coffee for breakfast 我早上总是喝咖啡（我总是喝咖啡当早餐）
         2. 表不变的真理及事实
            - The earth goes around the sun. 地球围绕太阳转
         3. 表示眼前的动作或状态
            - Here comes the bus. 公车来了
         4. 表确定的未来，计划（因为确定的未来相当于是 真理或事实，那么就可以当做第二条准则使用）
            - 一定要是明确的，计划，确定的 未来
            - Tomorrow is Mother's Day. 明天是母亲节
         5. 主要子句为未来式时，表时间，条件的副词子句用现在式 
            1. The birds will fly south when winter come. 冬天鸟会飞到南方
            2. What will consumers do if prices rise? 如果涨价了，消费者会怎样
   
      2. 过去式
         - 表明过去的动作或状态
            - These was a traffic jam on the expressway. 在高速公路上有堵车
         - 表示过去的习惯
            - I usually rode my bicycle to school when I was a school boy. 当我还是个学童的时候，我通常骑我的自行车去学校
            - We used to swim in the river. 我们过去习惯在这条河里游泳
         - 表经验，多随着 ever,never 等
            - I never heard from him before. 我以前从来没有他的消息
            - Did you ever see a panda? 你曾经看到过熊猫吗
   
      3. 未来式
         - be going to 表示未来式
            - I'm going to learn how to drive a car. 我打算学习如何开车
            - Are you going to sell that car? 你打算出售那辆车吗
            - My dog is very ill.I'm afraid he's going to die. 我的狗病得很严重，我怕他快死了
         - 注意：will 纯粹表示未来；be going to 表示未来要做的动作且经过事先的计划或安排（要到了的年龄不能用 be going to）
            - The telephone is ringing. --OK,I'll answer it. 电话在响，我来接
         - 一般现在式，现在进行式 表将来
            - Please take your seats;the performance is about to begin. 请就坐，演出要开始了
               - is about to （在时间很短暂的未来使用，即将发生的未来）
            - My father is taking us to the movies on Saturday. 周六，我的爸爸带我们去看电影
               - 现在进行式 表未来
               - 即将...；将要...
            - He was on the point of going out. 他在将要出门的时间点上
               - on the point of 在...的时间点上
            - The President is to make address. 总统将在今晚的电视上演讲
               - beV + 不定词 也可以表未来
   
      5. 现在进行式 => am/are/is + 现在分词(Ving)
         - 分词
            - 现在分词(Ving)
               - 动作进行
               - 主动
            - 过去分词(p.p.)
               - 动作完成
               - 被动
         - 举例
            - 现在正在进行的动作或状态
               - Where is Jack? -- He is playing tennis with Bob now. 杰克在哪里？-- 他正在和饱博打网球
               - Why are you driving so fast?You usually drive very carefully. 你为什么开得这么快？你通常开得很小心
               - John,you are being naughty. 约翰，你很调皮
            - 现在发生的反复的动作，多伴随者 always,all the time, constantly, repeatedly 等
               - Tom is always interrupting me when I'm talking. 汤姆一直打断我，当我讲话的时候
                  - 这种情况 always 通常翻译为“一直，老是”
               - You're constantly making excuses. 你一直在找借口
            - 表示未来
               - He is dying. 他要死了
               - They are opening a new boutique at the street corner. 他们要在街角开一家新的精品店
            - 表示心理，思考，感情，感官，形成等动词，不可用于进行式
               - 你正在看什么？
                  - What are you looking at? (O)
               - I am loving you. (x)
                  - 因为喜欢不能是进行式，不然会以为喜欢上了后马上就不喜欢了，但是在一些标语广告中可能会有这种进行式
               - What are you seeing. (x)
                  - see 是眼睛的基本功能，而且相对来说时间较短暂，所以不能用进行式，进行式是需要时间比较长的才行
                  - 所以应该用 watching 或 looking at
               - 我现在有只新表
                  - I am having a new watch now. (x) （不需要现在进行式，因为拥有了手表，下一秒一定有，而进行式会造成下一秒可能没有的情况，所以错误）
                  - I have a new watch now. 我现在有只新的手表

      6. 过去进行式 => was/were + 现在分词
         - 表示过去某一时间点正在进行的动作
            - I was washing dishes when my wife came home. 当我妻子回家时，我正在洗盘子
            - They were suffering from influenza. 他们患有流行性感冒
         - 表示过去习惯性的行为
            - At a teenager,he was always causing trouble for others. 在青少年，他老人给别人制造麻烦
            - In those days,we were getting up at seven o'clock. 在那些日子，她在七点钟起床
         - 以过去某一个时间点为基准，可确定的未来或计划
            - I thought you were coming home at six. 我认为你要在六点钟回来
            - He was coming to see me yesterday,but he didn't. 他昨天要去看你，但是他却没有
         - 表示过去反复的动作，常伴随 continually,constantly 等
            - She was constantly seeking the topic for a novel. 那个时候她一直在寻找写小说的题材

      7. 未来进行式 => will be Ving
         - 表示未来某一时间点正在进行的动作
            - I'll be driving at this time tomorrow. 我在明天的此刻会驾驶
            - I'll be waiting for you at 3 o'clock tomorrow afternoon. 明天下午3点我会等你
         - 表示最近的将来预定要做的动作（现在少用）
            - I'll be visiting London the day after tomorrow. 后天我会参观伦敦

      8. 现在完成式 => has/have + p.p.
         - 一些不规则变化的举例
            - ABC型
               - drink-drank-drunk
               - break-broke-broken
               - rise-rose-risen（升起，举起）（这个是不及物动词）
            - ABB型
               - raise-raised-raised（升起，举起）（这个是及物动词）
               - buy-bought-bought
               - sleep-slept-slept
               - feed-fed-fed
            - ABA型
               - come-came-come
               - become-became-become
               - run-ran-run
            - AAA型
	       - cost-cost-cost
	       - hit-hit-hit
	       - set-set-set
            - 特别注意的动词三态
               - fall-fell-fallen
               - fell-felled-felled
               - feel-felt-felt
               - find-found-found（找，寻找）
               - fine-fined-fined
               - found-founded-founded（建立，成立）
               - lie-lied-lied
               - lie-lay-lain
               - lay-laid-laid
               - see-saw-seen
               - saw-sawed-sawn/sawed
               - sew-sewed-sewed/sewn
               - fly-flew-flown
               - flee-fled-fled
               - flow-flowed-flowed
               - hang-hung-hung
               - hang-hanged-hanged
               - shine-shone-shone
               - shine-shined-shined
               - bind-bound-bound
               - bound-bounded-bounded
               - wind-wound-wound
               - wound-wounded-wounded
            - 使用时机
               - 表示从过去持续到现在的动作
                  - I have known Paul since we were children.
                  - 好久不见
                     - I haven't seen you for a long time.（for a long time 可以替换为 for years/ages）
                     - It has been a long time since I last saw you.
               - 表示动作或事件的完成
                  - I've just finished the work. 我刚刚完成了这个工作
               - 表示经验
                  - I have visited New York twice. 我参观过纽约两次
               - 现在完成式及过去式的不同
                  - My brother went to China yesterday. 我哥昨天去了中国（人已经回来了）
                  - My brother has gone to China. 我哥哥去了中国（现在不在这里，在去中国的路上或已经到了中国）
                  - I have lost my pen so I have to buy one.
                  - I lost my pen
               - 表示未来的副词子句中
                  - Wait till I've finished my coffee. 等我喝完咖啡
                     - Wait 其实已经有未来的效果了，作副词
                     - 后面的内容是时间
                  - As soon as I have saved 200,000 dollars,I'll buy a new car. 我存到20万美元，我就会买一辆新车

      9. 过去完成式 => had + p.p.
         - 表示到过去某一时间点为止动作或状态的持续及完成
            - The game had already begun when we arrived at the statium. 当我到达体育场时，比赛已经开始了
         - 表过去一段时间中的经验
            - I had never spoken to a foreigner before I got into university. 我进入大学之前，我从未和外国人说过话
            - She told me the story of the opera because she had seen it before. 她告诉我这部歌剧的故事，因为在之前她看过这部歌剧
         - 表比过去某时间点更早之前的动作
            - I lost the watch which my uncle had bought for me. 我弄丢了我叔叔买给我的手表
            - I didn't know that the band had broken up. 我不知道乐队解散了
         - 若纯粹两件过去的事，可用过去式（不要求先后顺序的情况下）
            - My uncle bought a watch for me and I lost it. 我叔叔买了个手表给我，而我把它弄丢了
            - The band broke up but I didn't know that. 这个乐园已经解散，但是是我不知道

      10. 未来完成式 => will have p.p.
         - 到未来某时间点前，可预测结果
            - The concert will have finished by the time we get there. 我们到那里，音乐会才结束
            - The lake will have frozen by tomorrow morning. 明天早上，这个湖会结冰
         - 表示在未来某时间点前可预测的经验或持续的状态
            - I will have failed the driving test three times if I fail tomorrow. 如果明天失败了，我会驾测失败
               - if 条件句如果是配合 未来的主句，那么条件句 可以直接用 一般式
            - You will have studied English for six years by the time you finish high school. 在你完成中学之前，你的英语会学满六年

      11. 完成进行式 => have/has + been + Ving
            - 表从过去某一时间点到现在为止会可能再持续或反复的动作
               - I have been doing this puzzle for 20 minutes. 我已经拼图20分钟了
               - How long have you been waiting here? 你在这里等多久了
               - I have just read through Tolstoy's War and Peace. 我刚刚读了托尔斯泰的战争与和平（我已经看完了，因为有 through 表示是通读，即读完了）
                  - I have been reading Tolstoy's War and Peace. 我通读了托尔斯泰的战争与和平（我从过去看到现在，读没读完不清楚，可能还会继续进行下去）

      12. 过去完成式 => had been Ving
         - 从过去的以前到去过，再进行下去
            - They had been searching for six months,when they found the treasure. 当他们找到宝藏时他们搜索了六个月（可能还会继续搜下去）
            - we had been going to paris for advanced study,but we never went. 我们早就打算去巴黎留学，但我们从未出发

      13. 未来完成进行式 => will have been Ving
         - You will have been studying English for five years by next March. 到明年三月你英语就学满五年了
         - She will have been teaching Japanese for ten years by next April. 到明年四月她就教日语十年了

   - 时态一致和叙述法
      - 过去往未来预测，那么那个未来还是在过去，不会跨到现在（依据叙述不能往后跨越一个阶段），只不过比过去更靠未来一点
      - 时态的一致
         - 例子1
            - My sister knows that I love the girl. 我姐姐知道我喜欢这个女孩
            - My sister knows that I loved the girl. 我姐姐知道我喜欢过这个女孩
            - My sister knows that I will fall in love with the girl. 我姐姐知道我会爱上这个女孩
         - 例子2
            - My sister knew that I loved the girl. 我姐姐当时知道我喜欢那个女孩
            - My sister knew that I had loved the girl. 我姐姐当时知道我喜欢过那个女孩
            - My sister knew that I would fall in love with the girl. 我姐姐当时知道我会喜欢上那个女孩
         - 例子3
            ```
            - She says                        she is free now.
            - She has said        that        she was free yesterday.
            - She will say                    she has been free lately.
                                              she will be free tomorrow.
                                              she had been busy before.
            ```
         - 时态的例外
            - 不变的真理 -> 现在式
               - The child learned that the earth goes round the sun. 这个小孩知道过地球是绕太阳转
                  - 前面是 过去式，但是后面是 一般现在式，两者时态有异，但因为后面是真理所以此句ok
                  - 不管前面半句时态是什么，后面的时态都应该是 一般现在式，因为是真理
               - The teacher told us that pratice makes perfect. 这个老师告诉我们练习会熟能生巧
            - 到现在都没有变的习惯或事实 -> 现在式
               - She often told me that she keeps early hours. 她经常告诉我她保持早睡早起
                  - 因为保持早的小时，说明，早晚都在保持，所以是“早睡早起”
               - She told me that school begins at eight. 她告诉我学习的活动八点开始
                  - 不可能每个学校都是在八点开始，而且这里的 school 是抽象的，所以只能是学校内部的活动
            - 历史的事实 -> 一般过去式
               - The teacher said that Columbus discovered America in 1492. 哥伦布是在 1492 年发现新大陆的
               - He said that World in War 2 ended 1945. 她说过 第二次世界大战是在 1945年结束的
            - 假设语气 -> 不受时态一致的限制
               - If he were a bird,he could fly. 如果他是一只鸟，他就能飞（纯假设语气）
               - He says/said if he were a bird,he could fly.（前面不管什么时态，假设语气不受时态一致的影响，假设语气该什么时态自己就什么时态）
               - He speaks English as if he were a native speaker. 他说英语像英语是他母亲一样（他说英语像他是个本地说话者一样）
                  - as if 宛如
                  - 假设语气，不受时态一致影响
               - He spoke English as if he were a native speaker.他说英语像英语是他母亲一样（他说英语像他是个本地说话者一样）
                  - as if 宛如
                  - 假设语气，不受时态一致影响

      - 叙述法
         - 举例
            - Bill says,"I hate math."（直接叙述法）
            - Bill says (that) he hates math.（间接叙述法）
               - 间接叙述法需要把内容的时态描述为应该所在的时态

         - 直接叙述法及间接叙述法的不同
            - 时态的变化
                  1. May said,"I like listening to pop music." May说过“我喜欢听流行乐”
                     - May said that she liked listening to pop music. May说过她喜欢听流行乐（间接叙述法需要配合时态一致）
                        - 时态一致，前面是过去式，在叙述她说也应该是过去式
                  2. The student answered,"An hour consists of sixty minutes."
                     - The student answered that an hour consists of sixty minutes.
                        - 一小时由六时分组成是不变的真理，所以后面只用一般式
                  3. Helen answered,"The rain has stopped."
                     - Helen answered that the rain had stopped.
                        - 由原句可知海伦说话发生在过去，而说的话又是在过去为中心的过去完成式
                        - 所以客观而言是过去完成式，在间接叙述时就应该用过去完成式表达

            - 人称代名词的变化
               1. She always says,"I don't like my hairstyle."
                  - She always says (that) she doesn't like her hair style.
                  - 注意 I 变成了 she
                  - 注意 don't 变成了 doesn't
                  - 注意 my  变成了 her
               2. I said to her,"I'm sorry you don't understand me."
                  - I told her (that) I was sorry she didn't understand me.
                  - 注意 said 改为了 told 并且 去年了 to
                  - 注意 am 改为了 was
                  - 注意 you 改为了 she
                  - 注意 don't 改为了 didn't
               3. She said,"I read this book."
                  - She said that she had read that book."
                  - 注意 第一句的 read 是过去式，第二句的 read 是完成式
                  - 注意 this 改为了 that

            - 时间，地点等的变化（直接叙述法 -> 间接叙述法）
               - now -> then
               - today -> that day
               - yesterday -> the day before / the previous day
               - last night -> the night before / the previous night
               - last year -> the year before / the previous year
               - tomorrow -> the next day / the following day
               - next week -> the next week / the following week
               - ago -> before
               - here -> there
         - 直接叙述句 -> 间接叙述句
            - 转变注意
               - 主词 say[said] to A,"直述句"
               - 主词 tell[told] A (that) 直述句
            - 概念
               - 主要子句的动词有时须改变
               - 补充连接词，代名词须改变
               - 间接叙述句的动词，须注意时态
               - 副词随内容做改变
            - 举例
               1. Mr.Wang said to me,"You will be able to get a free concert ticket at the charity bazaor tomorrow."
                  - Mr.Wang told me that I would be able to get a free concert ticket at the charity bazaor the next day.
                  - 注意 told, I, would, the next day
         - 直述句的间接叙述句
            - 转变注意
               - 主词 say[said] to A,"直述句"
               - 主词 tell[told] A (that) 直述句
            - She said,"I'm going to quit my job." 她说，“我打算辞掉我的工作”
               - She said (that) she was going to quit her job.
            - She said to me,"I can go to the movies with you tomorrow." 她说，“我明天可以和你去看电影”
               - She told me (that) she could go to the movies with me the next day"
         - 疑问句的间接叙述句
            - 疑问词问句 转变注意
               - 主词 + say(to A), "WH问句"
               - 主词 + ask(A) + 疑问词 + 主词 + 动词
            - 一般疑问句 转变注意
               - 主词 + say(to A), "Yes/No问句"
               - 主词 + ask(A) if(->whether) + 主词 + 动词
            - 疑问词问句
               - Tom said to her,"How can I get to your house from here?"
                  - Tom asked her (that) How he could get to her house from there.
               - My boss said,"who called me up this morning?"
                  - My boss asked (that) who had called him up that morning.
            - 一般疑问句
               - I said to him,"Are you going abroad?"
                  - I asked him whether he was going abroad.
               - He said to me,"Have you ever seen a panda?"
                  - He asked me whether I had seen a panda.
               - She said to the clerk,"Is this sweater knit by hand or by machine?"
                  - He asked the clerk whether that sweater was knit by hand or by machine
         - 祈使句的间接叙述句
            - 转变注意
               - 主词 say to A,"命令句"
               - 主词 tell A to v.
            - 词性
               - 命令 -> order,command 等
               - 要求 -> ask, beg, request 等
               - 劝告 -> advise 等
               - 提议 -> suggest, propose 等
               - 禁止 -> forbid, prohibit 等
            - 举例
               - Mother said to me"come back home by five."
                  - Mother told me to come back home by five.
               - My father said to me,"Don't give up your hope."
                  - My father told me not to give up my hope.
               - His secretary said to me,"Please call back after lunch."
                  - His secretary asked me to call back after luch, please.
                  - 因为直述句中有 please，有客气的成分，所以 把 told 改成了 asked
               - 注意：order,command,request,suggest 等时，其后常接 that 子句，而 that 子句中的 should 在美语中，通常省略
                  - I suggest that he (should) study hard. 我建议他应该用功读书
               - He said to me,"You should give up smoking."
                  - He advised me to give up smoking.
                  - 因为从语境中其实是 轻微的的语气，所以这里改为了 advised
               - She said,"Let's go for a walk."
                  - She suggested that we (should) go for a walk.
               - 重点：表示禁止的否定祈使句，用 forbid, prohibit 等
                  - The teacher said to us,"Don't leave your seats."
                     - The teacher forbade us to leave our seats. 这个老师禁止我们离开我们的座位
                     - The teacher forbade our leaving our seats. 这个老师禁止我们离开我们的座位
                     - The teacher prohibited us from leaving our seats. 这个老师禁止我们离开我们的座位
         - 感叹句的间接叙述句
            - 概念
               1. 感叹句中可加 very, really 等副词
               2. 动词可改为 cry,exclaim,shout,sigh 等
                  - cry：这里翻译为 大叫，大喊 等意思
                  - exclaim：惊呼，喊叫
                  - shout：喊叫，呼叫
                  - sigh：叹，感叹，欢息
               3. 伴随动词的副词有：gladly（快乐地）,regretfully（遗憾地）,bitterly（很苦闷地）,with joy,with delight,with relief 等
            - 举例
               - Ms.Lee said,"What a good idea you have!"
                  - Ms.Lee said that I had a very good idea.
                  - Ms.Lee shouted that I had a very good idea.
               - She said,"How convenient on-line shopping is!"
                  - She exclaimed with delight how convenient on-line shopping was.（结尾的标点也可以用 “!”）
                  - She said (that) on-line shopping was very convenient.（结尾的标点也可以用 “!”）
               - 重点：表祈愿时，和感叹句雷同，都是在加强情绪的表达，常用 pray,express 等动词
                  - He said,"May God help us!" 他说，“祈祷上帝能帮助我们”
                     - He prayed/expressed his wish that God might help them.
         - 合句的间接叙述句
            - and,but,or 等连接词所连接的两个对等子句，就称为合句
               - He said that she was sick and that she would go to a doctor.
                  - 这句的 and 是对等连接词，两个 that 是从属连接词，从属连接词不是对等连接词
                  - 第一个 that 可以省略，第二个 that 不能省略，因为隔得太远了，会让听者忘记起初的情况
            - 举例
               1. He said,"She is out,but she will be back soon."
                  - He said that she was out but that she would be back soon.
               2. The girl said to me,"these dancers arrived here yesterday,and they will perform on stage this evening."
                  - the girl told me that those dancers had arrived there the day before and that they would perform on stage that evening.
               3. 重点：对等连接词为 for 或 as 时，保留原连接词，不可用 that
                  - 因为 for 和 as 已经具有一定的意思，如果改成了 that 会意义损失
                  - Mom said,"Dad doesn't know it,as he has not heard of it." 妈妈说，“爸爸不知道那件事，因为他还没有听说那件事”
                     - Mom said that Dad didn't know it, as he hadn't heard of it.
               4. 重点：祈使句，and（或 or）...的间接叙述句仍保留and, or
                  - He said to me,"Get up at once,or you will be late." 他对我说，"立即起床，否则你会迟到"
                     - He told me to get up at once,or I would be late.
                     - He told me that I would be late unless I got up at once.
                     - He told me if I got up at once,I would not be late.
                  - She said to me,"Wash my car,and I'll give you len dollars."
                     - He told me to wash her car, and her would give me len dollars.
                     - He told me if I washed her car,she would give me len dollars.
         - 复句的间接叙述句
            - She said to me,"I gave him a big box of chocalates because I like him."
               - She told me (that) she had given him a big box of chocaltes because she liked him.
            - Joe said to me,"Do you think that she will help me."
               - Joe asked me if I thought that she would help him.
         - 有两个句子时的间接叙述句
            - He said to Gruce,"You are late here again what have you been doing?"
               - He told Gruce that she was late there again and asked (her) what she had been doing
               - 注意：添加了 asked (her) 作两个句子的连接
            - He said to me,"Your face looks familiar.Have you ever been on television?"
               - He told me that my face looked familiar and asked (me) whether I had ever been on television.
            - "He went to the barber's an hour ago,"said his wife to me,"and I hink he will be back very soon.Will you please step in and wait?"
               - His wife told me that he had gone to the barber's an hour before and that she thought he would be back very soon and asked me to step in and wait.

* 连接词
   - 依形态分为：
      1. 简单连接词：and,or,but,if,when等
      2. 相关连接词：both~and~,either~or~, not only~ but also ~
      3. 片语连接词：as soon as, as well as,even if 等
      4. 由其他词类转换而成mmediately,supposing：
   - 依功能分为：
      - 概念
         1. 依功能分为：将字与字，片语与片语，子句与子句等 连续一起
         2. 从属连接词：引导名词子句或副词子句的连接词
      - 对等连接词
         1. and（和；并且；那么）
            - Soldiers moved quickly and quietly. 士兵迅速又安静地移动
            - The book is of use and of interest. 这本书既有用又有趣
               - of + n. => adj.
            - Everybody sat down and the meeting began.
            - Hurry up,and you'll be in time for the train.
               - 前面半部分是祈使句，且是省略了主句等情况，所以 and 可以进行连接两个句子
            - There are magazines and magazines in that bookstore.
            - Go and (buy) some eggs.
            - 注意：在动词 come,go,see,try,write 之后的 and，可以 代替 to 不定式中的 to，即 Go to buy some eggs.
            - Bread and butter is my favorite at breakfast 奶油面包是我最喜欢的早餐
      - 相关连接词 
         - both~and~
            - He can speak English 和 He can speak French. 合并
               - He can speak both English and French. 英文和法文他都能说
               - He can speak English and French. 他能说英文和法文
            - Both he and I are senior high school students. 他和我都是高中学生
         - but（但是）
            - He was poor but happy. 他很贫穷但很快乐
            - Do it in haste but with caution. 赶快行动但要谨慎
               - with + n. => adv.
            - Excuse me,but could you tell me the way to the station? 对不起，你能告诉我去车站的路吗
               - 这里的 but 只是起了一个语气，明明打扰了别人，但是还是要打扰别人
            - 重点：相关连接词 not-but~（不是...而是...） 及 not only~ but also~（不仅...而且...）
               - He awns not one but two computers. 他拥有不是一个，而是两台电脑
               - She is not only wise but (also) kindhearted. 她不仅聪明而且善良
                  - She is both wise and kindhearted.
                  - She is wise and kindhearted alike.
                  - She is wise as well as kindhearted. 她即聪明又善良
                     - as well as 并且
            - 重点：下列句子中动词的单复数
                  - Both you and I are in the wrong.（bot and 的情况 动词是以 and 为准，and 肯定是复数）
                  - Not only you but also I am in the wrong（not only but also 的情况 动词以靠近的词作判断，这里即 but also 后面的 I 判断）
                  - You as well as I are in the wrong.（as well as 的情况，动词以第一个 as 前面，即 You 作判断）
         - or（或者；否则）
            - Do you want to go on foot or by bus? 你想步行还是乘公车去
            - This is a picture of an igloo or Eskimo snow house. 这是个雪屋即艾斯基摩人雪屋的照片
               - 这里的 or 翻译成 “即”
            - You had better take a taxi,or you'll your miss appointment. 你最好乘出租车，否则你会错过你的约会
               - had better 后面的动词 一定要是 原型
         - 重点：相关连接词 either~or~ 不是...就是...）和 neither / nor
            - either...or... 不仅仅是相关连接词，还是对等连接词
               - 动词以靠近的词为准，即 or 后面的
               - Either you leave the house or I'll call the police. 不是你离开这个家就是我报警
               - Either you or Jane is in the right. 不是你就是简是正确的
            - neither（也不） / nor（也不）
               - I've not visited the North Pole,neither/nor do I plan to.
                  - I have not visited the North Pole. 我没有参观过北极
                  - I don't plan to visit the North Pole. 我不打算参观北极
                  - 以上两句的二合一，并且有省略多余部分
               - Tom is not good at math. -- Neither/Nor am I. 汤姆不擅长数学，我也不擅长
               - 注意：neither或nor 为否定字，不可和not 连用，用倒装句
            - 相关连接词 neither~nor~ （既不...也不...）
               - neither~nor~ 的动词以靠近的词为主，即 nor 后面
               - The boy neither admits nor denies that he stole the bicycle. 这男孩既不承认也不否认他偷了脚踏车
                  - 注意 admits 和 denies 这里是 第三人称单数的形式
               - Neither my brother nor I have been invited. 我哥哥和我都没有被邀请
         - so（所以）
            - 只能连接两个子句
            - The buss broken down,so I was late (for school/work). 公车故障，所以我（上学/工作）迟到了
            - I practiced my speech hard,so I won a prize in the contest.我努力练习，所以能在演讲比赛中得奖
         - for（因为）
            - I am sleepy today,for I coundn't sleep well last night. 我今天很想睡觉，因为昨晚没睡好
               - I am sleepy today because I coundn't sleep well last night. 我今天很想睡觉，因为昨晚没睡好
               - 注意 because 是从属连接词，所以不需要逗号
            - because 是从属连接词
            - 注意：for（因为）只能连接两个子句，为较文章式的用法，口语中多用 because，但两者用法有差别
            - 重点：有些字原本是副词，但因和对等连接词一样可连接两个片语或子句，故称连接副词
               - 表 “选择” -> else,otherwise
               - 表 “相反，说明” -> however,nevertheless,on the contrary,namely,for example
               - 表 “结果” -> therefore,accordingly,hence
               - 表 “相连” -> also,besides,moreover,furthermore
               - 表 “相似” -> also,likewise,similarly
               - 表 “时间” -> then,meamwhile,at the same time
               - 表 “结论” -> in brief,in conclusion
               - 表 “加强语气” -> incleed,anyhow,in fact
               - 有时为了补充连接词的不足，也会和连接词一起
                  - and also,and therefore,and so,but still
               - I'm taking an umbrella with me;otherwise,I am going to get wet. 我有随身带伞，否则我会淋湿
                  - 如果 把 otherwise 改为 or 那么 “;” 应该改为 “,”
               - It may rain;nevertheless,we will start on our trip. 可能下雨，尽管如此，我们还是会开始我们的旅程
               - It rained that day;consequently the baseball game was called off. 那天下了雨，因此比赛取消了
               - She will come in half an hour;meanwhile,we will have coffee 她将在半小时后进来，在此同时，我们可以喝咖啡
               - His headache grew worse,but still he didn't complain. 他的头疼变得更坏了，但是他仍然没有报怨
      - 连接词和连接副词区别
         - 连接词：Gary is a nice person,but he has no friends. 盖伦是个不错的人，但是他没有朋友
         - 连接副词：
            - Gary is a nice person;however he has no friends. ~，然而他却没有朋友
            - Gary is a nice person;he has,however,no friends. ~，然而他有的却是没有朋友
            - Gary is a nice person;he has no friends,however. ~，他没有朋友，却
         - 从属连接词
            1. 引导名词子句
               - that
                  1. 当主词
                     - 他会成功。这件事是真的
                        - He will succeed.The thing is certain.
                        - That he will successed is certain.
                     - Bill 通过入学考试是真的
                        - That Bill passed the entrance exam is true. （这句话显得头重脚轻）
                        - It is true that Bill passed the entrance exam is true.
                     - That the world's climate is getting hotter is beyond any doubt. 世界气候正在变热是无庸置疑的
                       - It is beyond any doubt that the world's climate is getting hotter.
                  2. 当补语 => that子句放在 be 动词之后充当补语
                     - The trouble is that I cannot speak French. 麻烦的是我不会说法语
                     - 在口语中会省略 that，省略时，在原处加逗点
                     - 事实上他根本不可能关心我
                        - In fact is that he couldn't care about me in the least. 
                        - In fact is,he couldn't care about me in the least.
                     - 问题是，我身上没带钱
                        - The problem is that I have no money with me. 
                        - The problem is,I have no money with me. 
                  3. 当受词
                     - 当动词的受词 -> that 引导的名词子句，若接在 say,explain,hope,wish,know 等动词后，常省略 that
                        - I believe (that) he will do his best.
                           - I believe that thing. 结合 He will do his best.
                        - The radio said (that) today is the hottest day this summer. 收音机里报道说今天是今夏以来最热的一天
                        - He said (that) he would surely come and but that he might be ten or twenty minutes late.
                           - He said that he would surely come. 他说过他会来
                           - He said that he might be ten or twenty minutes late. 他说过他可能会晚10或20分钟到
                           - 注意 but 后面的 that，因为这两句都是他讲的，但是 but 连接了两个子句，要形成子句，所以是 but that
                           - 注意：动词之后有两个子句当受词时，第二个 that 不可省略
                        - 重点：不可接 that 子句作受词的动词
                           - He offered that he would drive me to the station. (x)
                           - He offered to drive me to the station. (O) 他提议载我到车站
                        - 重点：动词之后不能直接接 that 子句的有
                           - tell,inform,remind,assure,instruct 等
                              - He reminded that I had promised to help him. (x)
                              - He reminded me that I had promised to help him. 他提醒了我我答应过要帮助他
                        - 重点：主词 + suggest（建议）,advise（忠告）,order（命令）,reguire（要求） 等 + that + S + (should) + v.（that 不可以省略，should 可以省略）
                           - It be动词 + 形容词(necessary...等） + that + S + should + v. （that 不可以省略，should 可以省略）
                           - My mother insisted that my elder sister (should) arrive back before midnight. 我母亲坚持我姐姐应该在午夜前到家
                           - It is nessary that you (should) make up your mind. 你下定决心是必要的
                        - 重点：that 子句若在第5句型（S+V+O+C）中当受词时，须用虚拟词 it 代替
                           - 主词 + find,make,consider,thin,believe 等 + it + OC + that子句/Ving/to v.
                           - We consider that it is important to learn to make use of a dictionary. 我们认为学习使用字典是重要的
                              - We consider it important to learn to make use of a dictionary.
                                 - 稍微解析，it 和 important 之间没有 is 是因为 it 是受词，而不是主词，所以没有 is，以下两句同理
                              - We consider it important learning to make use of a dictionary.
                              - We consider it important we learn to make use of a dictionary.
                           - Many people find it strange that Americans move from place to place so often. 
                              - 许多人发现美国人经常搬家很奇怪
                           - I thought it rather odd that he hadn't come to the party which he had been looking forward to so much.
                              - 我认为他没有来参加他之前一直很期待的宴会很奇怪
                        - 重点： that 子句的同位格表现
                           - I'll see to it that the doors are all fastened. 我会看看门都是栓好了
                           - You may depend on it that we shall never give up. 你相信我们决不放弃
                              - depend on 后面如果根人，那么解释成“依赖”
                              - depend on 后面如果根事物，那么解释成“相信”
                           - He insisted on it that he was innocent. 他坚持他是无辜的
                           - I took it for granted that they would marry. 我把他们会结婚视为理所当然
                        - 注意：当介词的受词（仅限于 but,except,in 等）
                           - I don't deny but that they still insist on their opinions. 我不否认但他们仍然还一直坚持己见
                           - I remember nothing about her except that she wore glasses. 我不记得关于她的事情，除了她带眼镜
                           - I'm lucky in that I have three brothers. 我很幸运我有三个兄弟
                        - 当形容词的受词（仅限于一部分形容词）
                           - He is anxious that I will finish the work immediately. 他很焦迫我立即完成这个工作
                           - We were amazed that we saw you in townn. 我们很惊讶我们在镇里看到过你
                              - 等价：We were amazed at seeing you in town.

                  - whether / if（是否）
                     - whether,if 都能引导名词子句，但是 if 子句通常只当受词用
                        - 受词可以是连续的双受词形式，但不能是介词后面的受词，而且必须是肯定的情况
                        - She asked us whether/if we wanted to stay here (or not). 她问我们是否想要待在这里（这里可以用 if，相当于双受词的句型）
                        - Whether the report is true is questionable. 这个报道是否是真实的是 有疑问的/值得怀疑的（这里不能用if，因为是作的主词）
                           - 等价：It is questionable whether the report is true.（这里不能用if，因为是作的补语）
                        - The problem was whether we should call on ambulance at once.  问题是我们是否应该马上叫救护车（这里不应该用 if，因为这里是作主词的补语）
                        - It depends on whether they will appear. 这件事决定于他们是否会出现（这里不能用 if，因为是介词后面的受词）
                        - The question whether we have time to disscuss still remain. 我们是否有时间讨论的问题仍然存在（不能用if代替，因为这里是作同位格）
                           - 这里的 whether 不是形容词子句，而是同位格
                           - 这里 whether 是同位格，和 The question 是同位
                        - I don't care whether your car will break down or not. 我不介意你的车子是否会出故障
                           - 这里仍然不能用 if，因为前面是否定表现
                        - I can't decide whether to go or not. 我不能决定是否要去
                           - whether + to + v. 可以组成名词片语
                           - 等价：I can't decide whether I will go or not.
                        - Everyone wants to know:whether they will get a raise (or not). 每个从优都想知道他们是否会加薪
                           - Everyone wants to know whether or not they will get a raise.（这种情况一般是针对 是否... 的内容比较长的时候，所以提前用 whether or not 作前缀表述）
                           - Everyone wants to know if they will get a raise.
                           - get a raise 加薪

            2. 各种从属连接词的（副词子句）的意义
               - 从属子句
                  - 名词子句 - that+S+V，whether+S+V，疑问词+S+V
                  - 副词子句 - when+S+V,where+S+V
               - 表“时间”的从属连接词-when,as,while,after... 等
                  - 注意：as soon as,no sooner~ than~,hardly~when,scarcely~before,immediately,the moment...等（一...就...）
                  - As soon as she heard the bell,she turned over the test sheet. 他一听到铃声，她就翻开测验卷（这里的 heard, turned 是过去式）
                     - 这几个词组，不同的词组要求的时态也不一样
                     - She had no sooner heard the bell than she turned over the test sheet.
                        - No sooner had she heard the bell than she turned over the test sheet.
                     - She had hardly heard the bell when she turned over the test sheet.
                        - Hardly had she heard the bell when she turned over the test sheet.
                     - She had scarcely heard the bell before she turned over the test sheet.
                        - Scarcely had she heard the bell before she turned over the test sheet.
                     - Immediately she heard the bell,she turned over the test sheet.
                     - The moment she heard the bell,she turned over the test sheet.
                  - 直到许多天后，我才得知真相
                     - I didn't learn the truth until/till many days had passed.
                     - It was not until many days had passed that I learned the truth. 
                  - Once you decide to do it,please concentrate on it. 一旦你决定做，请全神贯注
                  - Every time I see Jane,I am reminded of her mother. 每次我看见Jane,我就想起她母亲

               - 表“地点”的连接词
                  - You may go wherever you like. 你可以去你喜欢的地方（wherever = anywhere that）
                  - Where there is a will,there is a way. 有志者，事竟成（有意志的地方就会有路）

               - 表“原因；理由”的从属连接词
                  - Because Mary refused his offers,Tom was in no mod to spend weekend. 因为 Mary 拒绝他的要求，Tom失去了欢度周末的心情
                  - Since you can't come,we had better asked for someone else for help. 既然你不能来，我们只好向别人寻求协助了
                  - As I was exhausted,I went to bed early. 因为我太累了，所以很早就睡了
                  - 例子 
                  ```
                    In the United States,the front seat next to the driver is considered the best in a private car,
                    partly because the driver is likely to be the host himself,and partly because the front windows offers the best view.
                  ```
                     - 在美国，私家车中驾驶旁的前座被认为是最好的，部分因为司机本身是主人，部分原因是前窗提供一个比较好的视野
                  - I don't like her（语气上昂） because she is conservative. 
                     - 等价：I like her but it is not because she is conservative. 我喜欢她但是不是因为她很保守
                  - I don't like her（语气下降） because she is conservative.
                     - 等价：I don't like her,Because she is conservative. 我不喜欢她，因为她太保守了
                  - Now (that) you mention it,I do remember. 现在你提到这件事情，我就真的记起它来了
                  - Seeing (that) you do not know the fact youself,we can do nothing to help you. 你自己都不知道事实，我们做不了任何事来帮你
               - 表“目的”的从属连接词
                  - He worked hard (so) that he might pass the exam. 他用功，那么就会通过考试
                     - 等价：He worked hard,so he pass the exam. 他用功，那么就会通过考试
                  - I got up early so that I could catch the first train. 我起得早，以至于我能赶上第一班火车
                     - I got up early to catch the first train. 我早起为了赶上第一班火车
                     - I got up early in so as to catch the first train.（so as to = in order to)
                     - I got up early in order that I could catch the first train.
                  - He walked coutiously lest he stumbled. 他谨慎地走，以免跌倒
                     - He wolked cautiously for fear he stumbled.（这种写法比较正式）
                     - He walked cautiously in case he stumbled.（这种写法比较口语化）
                     - 重点 so...that... 及 such...that... 表示“结果”（如此...以至于...）
                        - 他是如此勤奋的男孩以至于所有老师都夸奖他
                           - He is so deligent a boy that all the teacher praise him. （so 作副词）
                           - He is such a deligent boy that all the teacher praise him.（such 作形容词）
                        - I was such a fool that I complied with his request. 我如此地笨以至于我遵守了他的要求
                           - I was such a fool as to comply with his request. 我如此地笨以至于我遵守了他的要求
               - 表“让步”的的从属连接词
                  1. 主要子句 - 副词子句 时态对照表
                     - 现在式 - 现在式
                     - 过去式 - 过去式
                     - 未来式 - 现在式
                  2. Though/(Although) I was very tired,I went on working. 虽然我非常累了，我仍继续工作
                     - though/Although 和 but 不能同时使用（和 because 和 so 不同同时使用是一个道理）
                  3. Even if(=>though) you don't like cheese cake,try a piece of this. 即使你不喜欢乳酪蛋糕，还是吃一片吧
                  4. 无论下次选择输赢，我都将底支持他到底
                     - Whether he wins or loses at the next election,I'll support him to the very end.
                  5. Wherever/(No matter where) he goes,he alwasy takes an umbrella with him. 无论他去哪里，他总是随身携带一把伞
                     - 表示现在的习惯可以用一般现在式
                  6. No matter how hard you try,you won't succeed. 无论你多努力，你都不会成功
                  7. Young as he is,he is an able man. 虽然她很年轻，但他是个有能力的人
                     - 这里的 as 翻译为 “虽然”
                     - Though he is young,he is an able man. 虽然她很年轻，但他是个有能力的人
                  8. Teacher as she is,she cloes not like small children very much. 虽然她是个老师，但她非常不喜欢小孩
                     - 这里 Teacher 是 she is 的受词，放在前面不需要加冠词
               - 表“比较”的从属连接词
                  - I am usually as busy as I am now. 我通常像我现在一样忙
                  - I did not study so hard in my youth as you do now. 我在青年时没有像你现在这样那么努力
                  - You must read as many books as you can possible. 你必须尽可能地读许多书
                  - I'm three times as rich as you,and ten times as handsome as you. 我比你富三倍并且比你英俊十倍
                  - The weather was worse than we had expected. 天气比我期望的还差
               - 表“样态”的从属连接词
                  - Do in Rome as the Romans do. 入境随俗（像罗马人一样做）
                  - As you sow so,so shall you reap. 一分耕耘一分收获（你怎么播种就怎么收获）
                  - As the lion is the king of beasts,so the eagle is the king of birds. 因为狮子是百兽之王，所以鹰是百禽之王
               - 表“范围“的从属连接词
                  - As far as I know,he has nothing to do with the matter. 就我所知，他和这件事毫无关系
                     - have ~ to do with + O（谁和什么有关系）
                     - have much to do with + O（谁和什么有很大关系）
                     - have nothing to do with + O（谁和什么没有关系）
                  - As far as the eyes could reach,the city was a sea of fire. 放眼望去，这个城市陷于一片火海
                  - As far as I'm concerned,you can stay out all night. 以我而言，你可以呆在外面过夜
                  - As long as there were books and stationary,he never felt lonely. 只要有书和文具的陪伴，他就不会觉得寂寞
                     - As long as 这里翻译为“只要”
                  - He went on talking as long as three hours. 他持续讲了三个小时
